```python
# åç«¯å®ç°ç¤ºä¾‹: ä»£ç è§£æå™¨

import ast
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
from watchfiles import awatch
import libcst as cst

@dataclass
class GraphNode:
    """è§£æå‡ºçš„å›¾èŠ‚ç‚¹"""
    id: str
    name: str
    func_name: str
    line: int
    
@dataclass
class GraphEdge:
    """è§£æå‡ºçš„å›¾è¾¹"""
    source: str
    target: str
    condition: str | None = None

class LangGraphParser:
    """LangGraph ä»£ç è§£æå™¨"""
    
    def parse_file(self, file_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """è§£æ Python æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œæå– StateGraph ç»“æ„"""
        with open(file_path) as f:
            source = f.read()
        
        tree = ast.parse(source)
        nodes, edges = [], []
        
        for node in ast.walk(tree):
            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):
                # è§£æ graph.add_node("name", func)
                if self._is_add_node(node):
                    nodes.append(self._parse_add_node(node))
                # è§£æ graph.add_edge("from", "to")
                elif self._is_add_edge(node):
                    edges.append(self._parse_add_edge(node))
                # è§£æ graph.add_conditional_edges(...)
                elif self._is_conditional_edge(node):
                    edges.extend(self._parse_conditional_edges(node))
        
        return self._to_react_flow(nodes, edges)
    
    def _to_react_flow(self, nodes: List[GraphNode], 
                       edges: List[GraphEdge]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """è½¬æ¢ä¸º React Flow æ ¼å¼"""
        return {
            "nodes": [
                {
                    "id": n.id,
                    "type": "custom",
                    "position": {"x": i * 200, "y": 100},
                    "data": {"label": n.name, "func": n.func_name}
                }
                for i, n in enumerate(nodes)
            ],
            "edges": [
                {
                    "id": f"{e.source}-{e.target}",
                    "source": e.source,
                    "target": e.target,
                    "label": e.condition
                }
                for e in edges
            ]
        }


class LangGraphCodeGen:
    """LangGraph ä»£ç ç”Ÿæˆå™¨ (ä½¿ç”¨ LibCST ä¿ç•™æ ¼å¼)"""
    
    def add_node(self, file_path: str, node_name: str, func_name: str):
        """æ·»åŠ èŠ‚ç‚¹åˆ°ä»£ç """
        source = Path(file_path).read_text()
        tree = cst.parse_module(source)
        
        # ä½¿ç”¨ LibCST transformer æ·»åŠ  add_node è°ƒç”¨
        transformer = AddNodeTransformer(node_name, func_name)
        new_tree = tree.visit(transformer)
        
        Path(file_path).write_text(new_tree.code)
    
    def add_edge(self, file_path: str, source: str, target: str):
        """æ·»åŠ è¾¹åˆ°ä»£ç """
        # ç±»ä¼¼å®ç°...
        pass


async def watch_project(project_path: str, callback):
    """ç›‘å¬é¡¹ç›®ä»£ç å˜æ›´"""
    async for changes in awatch(project_path):
        for change_type, path in changes:
            if path.endswith('.py'):
                callback(path)
```

## ä¹ã€å¼€å‘ç¯å¢ƒé…ç½®

### 9.1 ç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡

```bash
# .env.example

# ========================
# åº”ç”¨é…ç½®
# ========================
APP_ENV=development
DEBUG=true
SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key

# ========================
# æ•°æ®åº“
# ========================
DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/ai_agent
REDIS_URL=redis://localhost:6379/0
QDRANT_URL=http://localhost:6333

# ========================
# LLM é…ç½®
# ========================
OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-xxx
ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=sk-ant-xxx
DEFAULT_MODEL=claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022

# ========================
# Agent é…ç½®
# ========================
AGENT_MAX_ITERATIONS=20
AGENT_MAX_TOKENS=100000
HITL_ENABLED=true
HITL_INTERRUPT_TOOLS=run_shell,write_file,delete_file

# ========================
# æ²™ç®±é…ç½®
# ========================
SANDBOX_ENABLED=true
SANDBOX_TIMEOUT=60
SANDBOX_MEMORY_LIMIT=512m
```

### 9.2 Docker Compose

```yaml
# deploy/docker/docker-compose.yml

version: '3.8'

services:
  frontend:
    build:
      context: ../..
      dockerfile: deploy/docker/Dockerfile.frontend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - backend

  backend:
    build:
      context: ../..
      dockerfile: deploy/docker/Dockerfile.backend
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://postgres:postgres@postgres:5432/ai_agent
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0
      - QDRANT_URL=http://qdrant:6333
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - redis
      - qdrant
    volumes:
      - ../../data:/app/data

  celery:
    build:
      context: ../..
      dockerfile: deploy/docker/Dockerfile.backend
    command: celery -A app.workers.celery_app worker -l info
    depends_on:
      - backend
      - redis

  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: postgres
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
      POSTGRES_DB: ai_agent
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"

  qdrant:
    image: qdrant/qdrant:latest
    volumes:
      - qdrant_data:/qdrant/storage
    ports:
      - "6333:6333"

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
  qdrant_data:
```

### 9.3 å¿«é€Ÿå¯åŠ¨

```bash
# 1. å…‹éš†é¡¹ç›®
git clone https://github.com/xxx/ai-agent.git
cd ai-agent

# 2. å¤åˆ¶ç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡
cp .env.example .env
# ç¼–è¾‘ .env å¡«å…¥ API Key

# 3. å¯åŠ¨æ‰€æœ‰æœåŠ¡
docker-compose -f deploy/docker/docker-compose.yml up -d

# 4. æ•°æ®åº“è¿ç§»
docker-compose exec backend alembic upgrade head

# 5. è®¿é—®
# å‰ç«¯: http://localhost:3000
# API:  http://localhost:8000
# æ–‡æ¡£: http://localhost:8000/docs
```

from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

app = FastAPI(title="AI Agent API")

# æ”¯æŒå¤šç§å®¢æˆ·ç«¯è®¿é—®
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # å¼€å‘ç¯å¢ƒ
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# RESTful API - Web å‰ç«¯ã€ç§»åŠ¨ç«¯
@app.post("/api/v1/chat")
async def chat(request: ChatRequest):
    ...

# WebSocket - å®æ—¶æµå¼è¾“å‡º
@app.websocket("/ws/chat/{session_id}")
async def websocket_chat(websocket: WebSocket, session_id: str):
    ...

# Server-Sent Events - æ›¿ä»£æ–¹æ¡ˆ
@app.get("/api/v1/chat/stream")
async def chat_stream(session_id: str):
    ...
